For each position, the ""native"" residue in the reference protein, the ""substituted"" residue in the superimposed protein and structural parameters are tabulated. 2- The data are filtered and grouped according to the ""native"" residue type, resulting in root clusters for classifications. 3- For each residue type, a hierarchical classification is achieved using a decision tree algorithm. Substitution scores are computed for all resulting clusters from residue distribution in the cluster.</caption><graphic xlink:href=""1471-2105-6-4-1""></graphic></fig><fig id=""F2"" position=""float""><label>Figure 2</label><caption>  Decision tree classification of all observed substitutions for Leucines. Similar trees are built for each of the 21 residue types, including half-cystine. The structural environment for a given cluster is defined by the edge labels along its path from the root cluster c<sub>0</sub>. For example, the nodes colored in gray indicate the partial classification path of a Leucine observed in a native structural environment whose descriptors s<sub>23</sub>, s<sub>15 </sub>and s<sub>10 </sub>verify s<sub>23 </sub>= pol = 3%, s<sub>15 </sub>= pac = 7% and s<sub>10 </sub>= d<sub>4 </sub>= 5.4A.</caption><graphic xlink:href=""1471-2105-6-4-2""></graphic></fig><fig id=""F3"" position=""float""><label>Figure 3</label><caption>  Evolution of the Mean Rank criterion averaged over Alanine residues at different tree depths. The annotator selects the boxes under each word in a gene/protein name and presses the "Mark" button. COMPUTATIONAL DETAILS  All computations are performed in the statistical computing environment <monospace>R</monospace> version 2.13.1 (<xref ref-type="bibr" rid="B14">R Development Core Team, 2011</xref>) with the packages flexmix 2.3-6, multcomp 1.2-7, survival 2.36-9, mvtnorm 0.9-9991, modeltools 0.2-18, latice 0.19-33, grid 2.13.1, tools 2.13.1. The EM algorithm for ML estimation of finite mixture models is implemented in the <monospace>R</monospace> package flexmix (<xref ref-type="bibr" rid="B6">GrÃ¼n and Leisch, 2008</xref>; <xref ref-type="bibr" rid="B10">Leisch, 2004</xref>). For mixtures of linear additive models with regularized estimation, <monospace>FLXMRmgv()</monospace> is used as model driver for the H- and M-step. <monospace>FLXMRmgv()</monospace> uses functionality for regularized fitting of generalized additive models from the <monospace>R</monospace> package mgcv (<xref ref-type="bibr" rid="B19">Wood, 2011</xref>). The datasets for the simulation study using artificial data were conveniently generated using functions <monospace>gcSim()</monospace> and <monospace>gcData()</monospace> from the <monospace>R</monospace> package gcExplorer (<xref ref-type="bibr" rid="B15">Scharl and Leisch, 2009</xref>). The yeast cell cycle dataset is available in the Bioconductor package yeastCC.CodeNumber:993   -   PMID:None   -   Acknowledgements  We would like to thank ISCB Executive Officer BJ Morrison McKay and ISMB conference organizer Steven Leard for logistic support and invaluable advice in organizing the symposium.
